      <div class="post post-24278 type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-bucketlists tag-bucket-lists tag-lists" id="post-24278">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        45 Amazing Things To Do Before You Die
       </h2>
       <div class="post-content">
        <p>
         In the past few years I have been to 30 countries, 5 continents and countless cities, all in the name of my bucket list.
         <em>
          And
         </em>
         in honor of my 45th (YIKES!) birthday today, I wanted to create a list of my favorite forty-fivebucket list checks from around the world.
        </p>
        <p>
         Hopefully, you will find bucket list ideas and inspiration from these
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span style="color: #808000;">
          <strong>
           45 Amazing Things to Do Before You Die
          </strong>
          .
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          <strong>
           <img alt="Annette White Bathing Elephants in Thailand | Bucket List Journey" class="alignnone wp-image-18924" height="426" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/IMG_7364-800x533.jpg" width="640"/>
          </strong>
         </span>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <span class="s1">
          <strong>
           1. Bathe Elephants at a Rescue in Thailand
          </strong>
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          In Northern
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/asia-destinations/thailand-asia-destinations/" target="_blank">
           Thailand
          </a>
          , an hour from
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/chiang-mai/" target="_blank">
           Chiang Mai
          </a>
          s city center, I spent a memorable day volunteering at the
          <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293917-d601884-Reviews-Elephant_Nature_Park-Chiang_Mai.html">
           Elephant Nature Park
          </a>
          . This is a special place where there was an eclectic bunch of Asian Elephants; some old, some young, some blind, some injured from working in the logging industry, some abused and some rescued from the circus. Not only were we able to feed these majestic creatures, but we also bathed them in the river.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          Read More &gt;
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2013/04/bathing-elephants-in-thailand/" target="_blank">
           Bathe Elephants at a Rescue in Thailand
           <br/>
          </a>
         </span>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2014/06/bucket-list-things-to-do-in-chiang-mai-thailand/" target="_blank">
          Bucket List of 18 Things to Do in Chiang Mai, Thailand
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          <img alt="Things to do before you die: Swim in Jellyfish Lake in Palau" class="alignnone wp-image-20611" height="480" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/jellyfish.jpg" width="640"/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          <span class="s1">
           2. Swim in Jellyfish Lake in Palau
          </span>
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Jellyfish Lake in the Micronesian country of
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/palau/" target="_blank">
          Palau
         </a>
         is home to millions of jellyfish that are deemedrelatively harmless since their stingis so light. It was still frightening for the first five minutes to be surrounded by jellyfish, some brushing up against my body. But, after the panic dissipated, this was one of my all-time favorite
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/my-bucket-list/" target="_blank">
          bucket list
         </a>
         travel adventures.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2013/10/jellyfish-lake-palau-micronesia/" target="_blank">
          Swim in Jellyfish Lake in Palau
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          <img alt="Things to do Before You Die: Visit an Orphanage in Africa" class="alignnone wp-image-20547" height="426" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/IMG_1108-800x533.jpg" width="640"/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          <span class="s1">
           3. Visit an Orphanage in Tanzania
          </span>
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.kibowaorphanage.com/">
          Kibowa Orphanage
         </a>
         is on the outskirts of downtown Arusha, hidden down a bumpy dirt road and painted in a friendly pale blue. There are 48 children that call it homeand,after four days onan
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2013/08/go-on-an-african-safari-in-tanzania/" target="_blank">
          African safari
         </a>
         in
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/africa/tanzania/" target="_blank">
          Tanzania
         </a>
         ,I spent a fun-filledafternoon with them. I chose to bringcolorful balloons, which could be turned into animals or creative hats. It was a joy to watch the children smile as they each made their favorite shapes.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2013/09/visit-orphanage-tanzania-africa/" target="_blank">
          Visit an Orphanage in Tanzania
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Things to do before you die: take a River Cruise" class="alignnone wp-image-24065" height="427" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/IMG_5963-copy-1024x683.jpg" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          4. Take a Christmas Market Cruise Along the Rhine River
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span style="line-height: 1.5;">
          For the holiday season,
          <a href="http://www.vikingrivercruises.com/" target="_blank">
           Viking River Cruises
          </a>
          and my traveling friend Cacinda of
          <a href="http://www.pointsandtravel.com/" target="_blank">
           Points and Travel
          </a>
          invited me to cruise along the Rhine River to visit festive European cities andalmost a dozen Christmas markets throughout
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/europe-travel-explore/germany/" target="_blank">
           Germany
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/europe-travel-explore/france/" target="_blank">
           France
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/europe-travel-explore/switzerland/" target="_blank">
           Switzerland
          </a>
          and the
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/europe-travel-explore/netherlands/" target="_blank">
           Netherlands
          </a>
          . Between the lighted cathedrals, festive markets and abundance of
          <em>
           <strong>
            glhwein
           </strong>
          </em>
          , I found my Christmas spirit again.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2014/12/take-christmas-market-cruise-along-rhine-river/" target="_blank">
          Take a Christmas Market Cruise Along the Rhine River
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          <span class="s1">
           <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="416" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/yx5PiPW7H8A" width="555">
           </iframe>
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          5. Create Your Own Summer Cocktail
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          <span class="s1">
           In the heat of the
           <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/arizona/" target="_blank">
            Arizona
           </a>
           Summer, I decided it was the perfect time to create my own refreshing cocktail. The funnest part? Testing all the different concoctions. In the end, my signature drink was a Lemon-Basil Fizz made with prosecco, coconut rum, raspberries, basil and lemon sorbet.
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;

        <h3>
         <strong>
          6. See the Changing of the Guard at Buckingham Palace in London
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Changing of the Guard at Buckingham Palace in Londontypically happens every other day (daily during the warmer months)at 11:30 amsharp. Get there early! Theguardsarrive by marching passVictoria Monument, directly in front of Buckingham Palace, and then entering through the ornate front gates of the palace. A mesmerizingshow follows, filled with band playing, synchronized marching and absolutely no smiles.
        </p>

         </a>

        <h3>
         <strong>
          12. Eat Worm Cakes in Hanoi, Vietnam
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          While taking a street food tour in
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/hanoi/" target="_blank">
           Hanoi
          </a>
          , there were lots of weird food to be eat, but the oddest was the worm cakes. On one street, anelderly woman had set up a propane, one burner stove to sell her fresh
          <i>
           <b>
            ragworm cakes
           </b>
          </i>
          , the live ingredients squiggling right next to the frying pan. The patties, about the size of a McDonalds hamburger, are a combination of worms, mandarin peel, dilland the chefs choice of spices. For just a dollar, the ownerfried them up fresh.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         They were flavorful, tasting more like a minced meat pie than what you would expect a dirty worm to taste like.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2014/12/eat-worm-cakes-vietnamese-street-food-hanoi/" target="_blank">

          13. Climb to the Peak of Sigiriya Rock in Sri Lanka
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>

         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/asia-destinations/sri-lanka/" target="_blank">
          Sri Lanka
         </a>
         . This UNESCO World Heritage siteis known for its beautifully landscaped gardens, well-preserved frescos and a crap load of stairs, all at different anxiety producing levels. Climbing the 1200 steps will take some stamina, but the view at the top will be totally worth it.
        </p>

         <strong>
          20. Experience Istanbuls Call to Prayer at the Blue Mosque

        <p>
         Five times a daythroughout the streets of
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/istanbul/" target="_blank">
          Istanbul
         </a>
         you can hear the trilling call to prayer, also known as
         <strong>
          e
         </strong>
         <em>
          <strong>
           zan
          </strong>
         </em>
         . During this time the voice of the bellowing
         <strong>
          <em>
           muezzin
          </em>
         </strong>
         , the man who calls the Muslims to prayer from a m
         <span id="ms__id300">
          inaret
         </span>
         , can be heard over the loudspeakers atdifferent mosques in the city. One of the best locations to witness this is while sitting on the benches between the Blue Mosque and Hagia Sophia. Powerful!
        </p>

         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/paris/" target="_blank">
          Paris
         </a>
         maynot be the largestCatholic cathedral in the world, but it just might be one of the most beautiful andfamous with an estimated 14 million visitorsa year. What will make your visit even more special is if you time it for when there is a mass. Its so powerful that it wont even matter that it is entirely in French. Plus, its totally
         <em>
          <strong>
           free
          </strong>
         </em>
         .
        </p>

        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          22. See the Mount Athos Byzantine Monasteries in Greece
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         Mount Athos is an
         <a href="http://whc.unesco.org/en/list/" target="_blank">
          UNESCO World Heritage
         </a>
         site located on the Easternmostfinger ofthe
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/halkidiki/" target="_blank">
          Halkidiki
         </a>
         peninsula in
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/europe-travel-explore/greece/" target="_blank">
          Greece
         </a>
         and there are 20 monasteries that call it home. Itis 363 square miles and there are 2,300 monks who live in this place dedicated to prayer and the worship of God.
        </p>
        <p>
         Men have to have special permission to visit this holy land, while womenmust keep their distance.
         <em>
          No exceptions.
         </em>
         But, womencan take a boat ride to witness it, as long as they stay 500 meters away.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2014/07/mount-athos-byzantine-monasteries-greece/" target="_blank">
          See the Mount Athos Byzantine Monasteries in Greece
         </a>

         <img alt="Things to do Before You Die: Take a Helicopter Ride to the Grand Canyon" class="alignnone wp-image-22347" height="426" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/05/IMG_6654-800x533.jpg" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          25. Take a Helicopter Ride into the Grand Canyon
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <span class="s1">
          After havingtraveled to
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/las-vegas/" target="_blank">
           Las Vegas
          </a>
          a half a dozen times in the past couple years, on this current trip I was looking for something more than sparkling lights,feathered girls and dancing water fountains. I wanted a unique Things to do Before You Die experience. A helicopter ride into the Grand Canyon fit the bill.
          <a href="http://www.sundancehelicopters.com/" target="_blank">
           Sundance Helicopters
          </a>
          took us 45 minutes from

          and landed us right into the Grand Canyon where we had time to explore and have a picnic.

          <a href="http://www.up-away.com/" target="_blank">

          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/galapagos-islands/" target="_blank">

          </a>
          : Blue-footed, Red-footed and Nazca. Though we didsee them all, my real bucket listgoal wasto witness aBlue-footed Booby mating dance. This dance was their uniquecourting ritual, which includedrocking side-to-side while lifting their eye-catching baby bluefeet.
          <em>
          </em>
          On our last day of exploring the
          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/galapagos-islands/" target="_blank">
           Galapagos Islands
          </a>
          , on North Seymour,we saw one very popular female birdsurrounded by a few maleBoobies who werestrutting their stufftrying to impress this desirable lady.

          <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/tokyo/" target="_blank">
           Tokyo
          </a>
          that squeezes in over200miniature bars into a network ofsix narrow alleys, made only forpedestrians.Most bars in this section of town seat less than ten drinkers and cater to the locals. But, it is possible to find somewhere the travelers are welcome and will flock to. I ended up doing most of my Golden Gai drinking atNessun Dorma, which means None Shall Sleep.

        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          29. Get Spooked at the Catacombs in Paris
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Catacombs in
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/paris/" target="_blank">
          Paris
         </a>
         , Franceis a labyrinth of caves underneath the heart ofthe cityand theresting place for the bones of six million Parisians.Starting in the late eighteenth century, remains were transferredto the ossuaryas overcrowded graveyards were closing due to the risk to the public. Though the underground maze is extensive, the portion that is open to the publicis a two kilometer Catacombs tour filled with skulls, bones &amp; stones. Traveling through these caves was creepily cool.
        </p>

        </p>
        <p>
         Though the
         <a href="http://www.giants.jp/top.html" target="_blank">
          Yomiuri Giants
         </a>
         at the
         <a href="http://www.tokyo-dome.co.jp/e/dome/" target="_blank">
          Tokyo Dome
         </a>
         draw larger crowds, you can also see the
         <a href="http://tokyoswallows.com/" target="_blank">
          Tokyo Swallows
         </a>
         play at the outdoor
         <a href="http://www.jingu-stadium.com/english/" target="_blank">
          Jingu Stadium
         </a>
         , which is what I did.

        <h3>
         <strong>
          31. Visit a Maasai Tribe in Tanzania, Africa
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         On the way back to the city ofArusha,after a long day on safari at Ngorongoro Crater in
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/category/bydestination/africa/tanzania/" target="_blank">
          Tanzania
         </a>
         ,our
         <a href="http://www.shadowsofafrica.com/">
          Shadows of Africa
         </a>
         driver took usdown a dusty, bumpy road to get toa Maasaivillage.We were greeted by the chiefs son and hewelcomed us into the inner circle of their living quarters, which consisted of abouteight smallhuts.There was one for each wife and their children, plus one for the husband who alternated which woman stays with him each evening. Not only was their polygamist lifestyle interesting, but so was their farming capabilities, minimalist living and culture.

           Paris
          </a>
          Pont des Arts bridge, near the Louvre, is a place where couplescanputpadlocks along the rails to secure theirlove. Then they throw away the keys so the love can not be unlocked. We bought a small goldlock, which had three keys attached, for five euros from abrilliant vendorwho stood at one end of the bridge.The merchanteven supplieda selection of colored markers to write our tender message with.

          Maui
         </a>
         ,the location where the kayak/snorkeling tour we had signed up for took place.This snorkling spot had been the center of numerous turtles sightings and the day we were there was no different. We were able to swim alongside several of these amazing creatures.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2012/08/searching-for-sea-turtles-sharks-in-olowalu/" target="_blank">
          Search for Sea Turtles &amp; Sharks in Olowalu
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Travel Bucket List: Have Afternoon Tea in London" class="alignnone wp-image-11490" height="631" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2012/05/IMG_1159-e1337895759997-1024x1009.jpg" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          44. Attend a Proper British Afternoon Tea in London
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         A proper Afternoon Tea in
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/london/" target="_blank">
          London
         </a>
         is aBritish tradition that I had no intention of missing out on. I like tea. And tiny little sandwiches. The
         <a href="http://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=4275&amp;awinaffid=215335&amp;clickref=&amp;p=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.agoda.com%2Froyal-garden-hotel%2Fhotel%2Flondon-gb.html%3Fasq%3DDaK1pGiY0by4RaqXCqEto03cYiB7W%252bjBPpjqQtb%252bwRqy%252byVeqh1mWbo0lRGq3J0YuCfpqFb%252ffx6yeOGhht9VQ8J7fgm7eyWUhdo%252bueG7cjxUaHthZDOtAQbLHbSivOxuQMbEGGi6uZkiZ9xEuzER2Xlk6OkbSRHkgg66d3UGkUz6vxtoAE6A7AAlXeY4QghJ6lyCsElX5bbinNYaKV0IlFjqMW3yFpypDsQXh2GlcAslB9Mod8LjV%252bw65lWjY4BLzg%252fWLET6PKLZqtPyFi%252bGUppvP0o%252bF%252fE7arx0Nquvf8e6GxA8czWpiZl%252bX%252fLPZgkB%252feWS9ChDbuhK8ckdCOoT2sJER%252fsx6E6pYFFykcYmPBDTlb8pNhwpQRQOTCTnByg0VeaxPisnwtGrqRDAzfMhlftaF4v4ae1QUUCmFsBS2p5BF7nrN2Q48XDXhFnJQx%252b4yP7Eb%252fQRfKoSksp2WZ7whA%253d%253d%20" target="_blank">
          Royal Garden Hotel
         </a>
         set up a traditionalAfternoon Tea in London at their Park Terrace restaurantfor us.Here we indulged in Pear Caramel and Chocolate Chip Truffle tea, along withsandwiches, sweets, scones and curd.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2012/05/a-proper-british-afternoon-tea-in-london/" target="_blank">
          Attend a Proper British Afternoon Tea in London
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Life List Idea: Participate in a Japanese Tea Ceremony at Happo-en" class="alignnone wp-image-20479" height="426" src="http://bucketlistjourney.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/IMG_2387-800x533.jpg" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         <strong>
          45. Participate in a Japanese Tea Ceremony in Tokyo
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.happo-en.com/english/index.html">
          Happo-en Japanese Garden
         </a>
         sits in Shirokanedaidistrict of
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/tag/tokyo/" target="_blank">
          Tokyo
         </a>
         and is an exquisite example of natural beauty with its ancient bonsai, koi pond and blanket of cherry blossoms in the Springtime. Not only is ita beautifulrepresentation of a Japanese garden, but you can schedule to participate in a traditional Japanese tea ceremony where you will be drinking
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matcha" target="_blank">
          Matcha
         </a>
         in their wooden Muan tea house.
        </p>
        <p>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2013/09/japanese-tea-ceremony/" target="_blank">
          Participate in a Japanese Tea Ceremony in Tokyo
          <br/>
         </a>
         Read More &gt;
         <a href="http://bucketlistjourney.net/2015/01/22-bucket-list-things-to-do-in-tokyo/" target="_blank">
          22 Bucket List Things to Do in Tokyo
         </a>
        </p>

               <a aria-label="Reply to Annette White" class="comment-reply-link" href="/2015/02/45-amazing-things-to-do-before-you-die/?replytocom=655639#respond" onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-655639", "655639", "respond", "24278" )'>
                - Reply
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text">
               <p>
                Hello, pretty lady! I have heard of El Camino de Santiago and that walk would be quite an incredible feat. If you end up doing it, Id love to hear about your journey.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </li>
